\hypertarget{classsamplePDFFDBase}{}\doxysection{sample\+PDFFDBase Class Reference}
\label{classsamplePDFFDBase}\index{samplePDFFDBase@{samplePDFFDBase}}


Class responsible for handling implementation of samples used in analysis, reweighting and returning LLH.

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Class responsible for handling implementation of samples used in analysis, reweighting and returning LLH. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{samplePDFFDBase_8h_source_l00023}{23}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{samplePDFFDBase_8h_source}{sample\+PDFFDBase.\+h}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fillArray()}{fillArray()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void sample\+PDFFDBase\+::fill\+Array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}



DB Nice new multi-\/threaded function which calculates the event weights and fills the relevant bins of an array. 

fills the sample\+PDFFD\+\_\+array vector with the weight calculated from reweighting

@function \mbox{\hyperlink{classsamplePDFFDBase_a0d6150d9e001bd6df8732bf2fd7480b9}{sample\+PDFFDBase\+::fill\+Array()}} Function which does the core reweighting. This assumes that oscillation weights have already been calculated and stored in \mbox{\hyperlink{classsamplePDFFDBase}{sample\+PDFFDBase}}\mbox{[}i\+Sample\mbox{]}.osc\+\_\+w\mbox{[}i\+Event\mbox{]}. This function takes advantage of most of the things called in setup\+SKMC to reduce reweighting time. It also follows the ND code reweighting pretty closely. This function fills the sample\+PDFFD array array which is binned to match the sample binning, such that bin\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} is the equivalent of \+\_\+h\+PDF2\+D-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}Get\+Bin\+Content(2,2) \{Noticing the offset\}
